    "ops.node(3, 0.0, 2.0)\n",

    "ops.node(24, 4.0, 3.0)\n",
    "ops.node(25, 4.0, 4.0)\n",
    "\n",
    "ops.nDMaterial(\"ElasticIsotropic\", 1, 1000, 0.3)\n",
    "\n",
    "ops.element(\"quad\", 1, 1, 6, 7, 2, 1, \"PlaneStress\", 1)\n",
    "ops.element(\"quad\", 2, 2, 7, 8, 3, 1, \"PlaneStress\", 1)\n",
    "ops.element(\"quad\", 3, 3, 8, 9, 4, 1, \"PlaneStress\", 1)\n",
